$ cat <<'EOF' > list_apt_files.py
from pathlib import Path

# Define the directory to list
apt_dir = Path('/etc/apt/')

# List all file paths recursively
for file_path in apt_dir.rglob('*'):
    if file_path.is_file():
        print(file_path.resolve())

EOF

import os

def list_files_in_directory(directory):
    try:
        for root, dirs, files in os.walk(directory):
            for file in files:
                print(os.path.join(root, file))
    except PermissionError:
        print("Permission denied: Cannot access some files in /sys/kernel/")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"An error occurred: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    list_files_in_directory("/sys/kernel/")
EOF
